碧庞皓环保技术(上海)有限公司 BMH ENVIRONMENTAL PROTECTION TECHNOLOGY (SHANGHAI) CO., LTD.
电话 Tel.: 86 21 6104 2222 网址 Website: www.bmh.fi 碧庞皓环保技术(上海)有限公司提供的霸王龙
(Tyrannosaurus)垃圾预处理系统，把固体废弃物 (生活垃圾、工业垃圾、商业垃圾等)经过破碎、分选 等工艺，处理成为高质量的、均匀的燃料(SRF, Solid Recovered Fuel,固体回收燃料，在欧洲是有标准的 燃料)，可以替代化石燃料，供循环流化床锅炉或水泥 窑使用。预处理工艺将所有垃圾破碎成80 - 100mm的 粒径，分选出含铁金属和有色金属，分选出不可燃的物 料，如玻璃、石头、陶瓷等等，生产出高质量的燃料。
The Tyrannosaurus waste pre-treatment system from BMH Environmental Protection Technology (Shanghai) Co., Ltd. turns solid waste (MSW, industrial and commercial waste), through the shredding and separation process, into high quality, homogeneous fuel (Solid Recovered Fuel, SRF, which has certain standards in the Europe). SRF is a replacement of fossil fuel and can be used by the CFB boiler and cement kiln. The target of the pre-treatment process is to reduce waste particle size into 80-100mm, separate the ferrous and non-ferrous metal, and separate the non-combustible fraction, such as glass, stone and ceramics to produce high quality fuel.
